Pkgs on Nix

Curated information about every package on Nix!

nixpkgs / erlang_nox - Erlang is a programming language used to build massively scalable soft real-time systems with requirements on high availability. Some of its uses are in telecoms, banking, e-commerce, computer telephony and instant messaging. Erlang's runtime system has built-in support for concurrency, distribution and fault tolerance.

Homepage - https://www.erlang.org/

License - Apache-2.0

Maintainers - Justin Wood - Oleksii Filonenko - Thomas Depierre - Gleb Peregud - Raphael Megzari - Eric Bailey
